<h2> <span class="mw-headline" id="General_Information">General Information</span></h2>
<div class="wi_body" style="width:100%">
<table border="0">

<tr>
<th class="wi_head">Work Title
</th>
<td class="wi_head" style="width:100%">Slavonic Rhapsodies
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th class="wi_head">Alt<span class="mh555">ernative</span><span class="ms555">.</span> Title
</th>
<td class="wi_head">Slovanské rapsodie
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th>Composer
</th>
<td><a href="/wiki/Category:Dvo%C5%99%C3%A1k,_Anton%C3%ADn" title="Category:Dvořák, Antonín">Dvořák, Antonín</a>
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th><span class="mh555">Opus/Catalogue Number</span><span class="ms555">Op./Cat. No.</span>
</th>
<td>Op.45&#160;; B.86
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th><span class="mh555">I-Catalogue Number</span><span class="ms555">I-Cat. No.</span>
</th>
<td>IAD 83
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th><span class="mh555">Movements/Sections</span><span class="ms555">Mov'ts/Sec's</span>
</th>
<td>3 pieces:
<ol><li> Allegro con moto (D major)
</li><li> Allegro ma non troppo—Moderato (G minor)
</li><li> Andante maestoso—Allegro assai (A-flat major)
</li></ol>
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th><span class="mh555">Year/Date of Composition</span><span class="ms555">Y/D of Comp.</span>
</th>
<td>1878
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th>First Perf<span class="mh555">ormance</span><span class="ms555">.</span>
</th>
<td>1878-11-17 in Prague (Nos.1 and 2)<br />1879-09-24 in Berlin (No.3)
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th>First Pub<span class="mh555">lication</span><span class="ms555">.</span>
</th>
<td>1879
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th>Dedication
</th>
<td>Baron Paul von Dervies
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th><span class="mh555">Average Duration</span><span class="ms555">Avg. Duration</span>
</th>
<td>39 minutes
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th><span class="mh555">Composer Time Period</span><span class="ms555">Comp. Period</span>
</th>
<td><a href="/wiki/Category:Romantic" title="Category:Romantic">Romantic</a>
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th>Piece Style
</th>
<td><a href="/wiki/Category:Romantic_style" title="Category:Romantic style">Romantic</a>
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th>Instrumentation
</th>
<td>orchestra <span class="expandline">
<dl><dd>2 piccolos*, 2 flutes, 2 oboes, 2 clarinets, 2 bassoons<br />4 horns, 2 trumpets, 3 trombones<br />timpani, bass drum, cymbals, triangle, harp*, strings<br />*<small>No.1 uses a single piccolo, No.3 employs 2, harp in Nos.2 and 3 only</small> </span>
</dd></dl>
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th>External Links
</th>
<td><span class="plainlinks"><a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://www.antonin-dvorak.cz/en/slavonic-rhapsodies">antonin-dvorak.cz</a></span>
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th>Extra Information
</th>
<td>Version history:
<ul><li> Composed for orchestra, 1878 (= B.86)
</li><li> Also arranged by Dvořák for Piano 4 hands. 1878 (= B.506)
</li></ul>
</td></tr></table>
